{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01ScmswEUNT4kZaZd1aPfdNP","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Now I understand the race condition better. Looking at the __wait_on_bit function:\n\n1. It calls prepare_to_wait to register on the wait queue\n2. It checks if the bit is still set (line 394)\n3. If the bit is set, it calls the action (which can return -ERESTARTSYS if a signal arrived)\n4. It loops back and checks the bit again (line 396)\n\nThe race condition would be:\n1. RPC reply arrives and clears the RPC_TASK_QUEUED bit\n2. At the same time, a signal arrives\n3. The action function (rpc_wait_bit_killable) returns -ERESTARTSYS\n4.
